<rating>5</rating><Text>Jumbo Rock Cafe' is an excellent example of why you shouldn't knock it till you try it. If it's your first time there, you may be a little confused walking into a Mobil gas station. The cafe/restaurant is located inside the back of the gas station.
However, I can assure you, you will not be disappointed! Jumbo Cafe has an amazing menu and is quite the neat little cafe. The food is above all, amazing!
I would highly recommend the Monument Burger. It is the best burger I have had from Twentynine Palms to Yucca Valley. I will update this review if I find something better.</Text><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOnJ_R5bMAoAsTbezLDAfrBpMWbJTC3VLBtt5Y=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipO4ewq3tEJQMBMTIEluUW-cqOdJm3G0CY9mRFI=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pictures><Response>None</Response><gmap_id>0x80dac0ad5afaaaab:0xadbf46143af5be01</gmap_id></record>

<rating>5</rating>< review>
Cute little cafe located in the back of the Mobil gas station. Doesn't sound appetizing? You would be so wrong!  It has a nice vibe, and the food and coffees are tasty! The food is American and Indian and very good! There are meat, vegetarian and vegan options, and having had a number of items on the menu, I can honestly say that everything I've tried has been superb in taste and freshness. They have an extensive coffee/tea listing as well. I like their coffees better than Starbucks! The taste of their coffees is so smooth, not acidic at all, probably due to the cold brew method. If you like to try a non-franchise eatery, this is the one! Oh, and they have also started making donuts. I had one Saturday  (they are large) and it was so good! Light, fluffy and delicious.</review>

< Name>
Brandon Steffenhauser</Name>
<UserId.>100294715472921607416<//UserId.><Rating>5<//Rating><Text>I wish there were a way to give 4.99999999 stars, so I will have to round up. I just took ownership of a 2017 Victory Octane and I have to commend Gary Saffle on providing the best motorcycle buying experience I have had - ever. I was referred by a friend who is chapter VP for the VMC and was given the VIP treatment every step of the way. Well, I thought it was the VIP treatment until I saw that others in the showroom were given the same level of care and detail to their questions, concerns, and shopping experience. Gary definitely deserves an award in my book. When I went to pick up my bike I received great help from Leo, as well.

What made this even better is my shopping experience for Victory did not start out great. I initially went to Mission Motorsports in Irvine and they were not helpful; I didn't feel like my business was valued, and overall like they couldn't care less if I decided to buy or not. At Indian of El Cajon Gary was very transparent on the pricing, fees, and breakdown of what my deal would look like - AND he was able to beat Mission's price and help me with a fantastic deal that even the CFO (wife) easily agreed with. I got 95% of what I wanted with this Octane and I'm excited to ride it, do fun-runs, group/club rides, and just cruise the beaches.

But why not a solid 5 stars? This is not to the fault of Gary or the dealership - but Victory. The accessories I wanted could not be acquired and no ETA could be easily determined. I was a bit disappointed to see a lack of support by the brand (Victory) to ensure that simple accessories like the Stage 1 Slip-On exhaust or Tachometer were so far behind on production that it would not make sense to "order" them if they could not be delivered WITH the bike for pick-up. Accessories make up a good margin for dealers and it would have helped both of us. For an Octane that is a "Performance Cruiser" these would be fantastic to "complete" my purchase. Now I will have to "wait" until they become available some time in 2017 and add them later.

Overall, I HIGHLY recommend coming here for a Victory or Indian. The staff was incredibly helpful and friendly. They treat you like one of the family and truly appreciate your business.<//Text></record>

< user_id>
106592247642803102520< /user_id>
<user_name>Bezimienny -<//user_name><date>1533585580898< /date><Rate>5< /Rate>< review>
I remember visiting Tommy's back in LA, for those special chili nights; what better place to go other than here?

For a restaurant deliciously notorious for their chili-adorned fast food (their "world famous chili burgers", in particular), the cleanliness and hygiene of the interior were superb. In fact, you wouldn't think the place was a 'slam-everything-in-chili-and/or-cheese' with how clean and spiffy the tables, chairs, windows, everything looked.

There's even a sanitizer dispenser right beside the napkin equivalent (tip: napkins are very essential when eating here). Like, damn.

The service is especially great. Staff here are nice and patient, though it might've been because we arrived at a not-so-busy time. Regardless, it definitely helped with my pleasant experience here.

To be fair, the food here should be something of a craving on certain days rather than an occasional thing. Although I rate the food 4 stars (the chili burgers back at LA were a bit better), the additional bonuses provided here bumps it up to a 5. Awesome.

tl; dr ++staff/service
++clean/sanitary
++AC (air conditioning)
+food and timing<//review>

<Gmap_id>0x80dcb86e19b65079:0xea342cafb4b4410f< /Gmap_id>< Review>
I've eaten tons of burgers. For some reason, when I first tried Tommy's, I didn't like the food at all. As I was driving past it, omw to In-&-Out, I saw In-&-Out's gigantic line. I was so hungry!!! I didn't have the time. So, I pulled over into Tommy's to order their California Classic without the chili. OMG, I fell in love. Their fat tomatoes, thick sweet pickles and onions... We found ourselves a champ! After a couple of visits, where we compare burger to burger, my boys will choose Tommy's about 55-60% of the time. Mostly, because we are so familiar with In-&-Out. Mind you, we don't hate In-&-Out - are you crazy?!? But, Tommy's, after traveling far down the In-&-Out road, is a welcome change. I prefer it most times now.<//Review>

Chili everywhere... Chili on this chili on that. Ultimate comfort food. Burgers are great. But the chili... Oh man. Not moms chili. Excellent place to go when you say "diet schmiet"... A must for any burger and chili fan.</Text>
